Store the same underlying storage implementations for resources across different API versions\\n4. The ResourceEncodingConfig determines which version is actually used for etcd persistence\\n5. The StorageVersion manager tracks which versions have been registered and synced\\n\\nThis architecture allows Kubernetes to serve multiple API versions (v1, v1beta1, v1alpha3, etc.) of the same resource while controlling which version is the canonical storage version through the ResourceEncodingConfig.\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
